FROM [Posts] AS [p]

2026-06-27 14:11:34.743 -04:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (1ms) [Parameters=[@__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[PostContent], [t].[ImageUrl], [u].[Username], [t].[UserId], [t].[CreatedAt], (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Comments] AS [c]
    WHERE [t].[Id] = [c].[PostId]), (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Likes] AS [l]
    WHERE [t].[Id] = [l].[PostId]), [u].[Id], [t0].[CategoryId], [t0].[Name], [t0].[PostId], [t0].[Id]
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[PostContent], [p].[UserId]
    FROM [Posts] AS [p]
    ORDER BY [p].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [t].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[CategoryId], [c0].[Name], [p0].[PostId], [c0].[Id]
    FROM [PostCategories] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c0] ON [p0].[CategoryId] = [c0].[Id]
